Spring and Autumn

Little Western Paradise

— By Zhang Henshui

Chapter 6: A Poor Girl Should Not Be Ashamed to Become a Teacher, and a Western Guest Is Not Worth Respecting, Only Humiliating a Humble Heart

If you don't think the method I've described is satisfactory, then he will still be named Zhu and I will still be named Jia. What else is there to talk about? When Yueying heard this, she realized that after being looked at for so long and having her hand touched, the other party wasn't necessarily going to take her. A poor girl has so little status. She felt a pain in her heart, and tears were about to stream down her face. However, Hu's wife didn't feel anything. She felt that this was how business should be done. She asked, "According to Master Jia, how should it be done?" Jia Duocai swayed his body, ready to say what he wanted to say, but he heard someone calling out, "Brother Jia, are you home?" Jia Duocai recognized the voice as Li Shilian's. So, he replied, "At home, at home." As he said this, he rushed out the door and stopped Li Shilian. He said in a low voice, "That little thing is in my room." Li Shilian narrowed his eyes and said with a smile, "You are really something. You actually got him first." Jia Duocai smiled and said, "Don't talk nonsense. There's still a woman with bound feet accompanying me in the room. We were just discussing the conditions." Li Shilian raised his head, hesitated, and pondered, "This is very inconvenient." Jia Duocai smiled and said, "What? Are you talking about the woman from yesterday? I stand corrected, I stand corrected." Li Shilian said seriously, "This is a serious matter, not a joke. Haven't two Germans just arrived in this Little Western Paradise? They came on the same train as me." Jia Duocai said, "What are you bringing up foreigners for?" Li Shilian said, "His Chinese assistant, Zhao Guofu, told me that the two Germans want to talk to you." Jia Duocai said, "Really? What do they want to talk to me about?" Li Shilian said, "I don't know. Since he specially asked me to inform you, there must be something they want to discuss. Why don't you talk to him? But you have a female guest in your room, so it seems inconvenient to have him come over now." (94)

In the Thick Fog

— Zhu Ying

Although it was only two days before the full moon, the fog covered the entire sea. Not only was the moonlight completely blocked by the fog, but even the strong searchlights could not reach beyond ten feet. The foghorn on the ocean liner kept sounding, but in the thick fog, it sounded like a child blowing a toy trumpet.

Xu Changxing's large sand boat was fully loaded with goods, heading from Tianjin to Shanghai. Although that night it had reached only twenty nautical miles from the Songkou, and they were preparing to work hard all night to catch the early tide to enter the port, the thick fog blocked the way.

The sea was a vast expanse of white, and had lost its spirit of serenity and majestic posture, although the water was still surging against the bottom of the boat. All thirty-odd people on the boat were focused on preventing accidents from happening, because according to the experience of veteran sailors, under such a heavy fog, misfortune could easily befall.

Sure enough, at the moment when half of the sun had just emerged from the water, the searchlight on an ocean liner suddenly broke through a fog wall that was a little more than ten feet thick and shone directly on Xu Changxing's boat. Although the ocean liner was traveling at a very low speed, in less than ten seconds, there was a loud crash, followed by cries and shouts for help. Xu Changxing's large sand boat, which had been sailing in the sea for more than ten years, was rammed into two sections by the ocean liner and completely sank to the bottom of the sea in half a minute. Floating on the surface of the water were only some planks, debris, and a few crew members whose faces could not be seen clearly.

By the afternoon of the next day, except for a dozen or so crew members who were rescued by the ocean liner and taken into port, the rest had been swallowed by the sea god, although their wives were still waiting on the shore, hoping to be rescued by another boat.

Tidbits

— (Jin Yang)

A person who does not admit their mistakes has no determination to change.

Before you jump, look around you in all directions.

A person who submits a manuscript but doesn't see it published suffers the same pain as an editor who doesn't receive good manuscripts.

The Smiling Leaf Sweeper

— Xin Ren

In the beautiful scenery of spring flowers and autumn moons, I have never seen such an old and hunched leaf sweeper on this tree-lined path. It wasn't until the second half of October, when the wisteria in front of the window turned into dragon-snake-like skeletons, and I could see the buildings outside the park directly from my room, that I felt that the years were already late in the winter monsoon. As if reluctant to part with the few remaining green leaves on the branches, I put on my clothes and walked to the open space next door. As I was gazing at the blue of the sky, I heard heavy footsteps echoing from the forest. Soon, I saw the old leaf sweeper. In his hand, he held a very large bamboo broom, standing upright almost longer than his bent body. On his long, silver-gray beard that hung down to his chest, I could see that he was already very old. He wore a French velvet hat that someone else had discarded, and a cotton-padded coat was wrapped in a woolen sweater that had lost its buttons. He was already wearing cotton shoes. Old people are more susceptible to cold than young people, but his fingers were still trembling, as if his clothes were not warm enough. I stood with him for a short time and began to talk.

"Old man, when did you start doing this job?" I asked. He didn't answer, but only smiled at me, as if he knew that I was asking with my eyes rather than with my ears. I continued to ask, "What's your name?"

"Where is your home?" He only responded with a smile. I went on to ask who was in his home, but he shook his head, indicating that there was no one.

"Then how much money can you earn each day?"

When he heard this question, he seemed a little excited. His silver-gray beard moved, as if he wanted to say something, but in the end, he didn't say a word. I couldn't help but feel a pang of sympathy in my heart and said, "Come, wouldn't it be good to rest at my place?"

So, this sentence aroused another smile from him, a bleak smile. He lowered his head, moved his heavy steps, swung the bamboo broom on the yellow leaves on the ground, and his bent body was illuminated by the sun, casting a bent shadow on the yellow leaves. ... He finally did not accept my invitation.

The years are indeed late. I sighed softly.

I went back home. It was dark. In the darkness, I still saw the leaf sweeper's smile.

Different Worlds

Scattered Strings

— (Ye Qibai)

Along the banks of the Huangpu River, there must be countless workers.

Along the bustling roads, there must be many bums.

Around every tram station, train station, grand hotel, restaurant, and company, there must be many rickshaw pullers.

Around every school, there must be many candy stalls.

Along both sides of every alley entrance, there must be tiger stoves and cigarette paper shops, and other shops.

Along the tram stops and other places, there must also be cigarette paper shops.

Imperial Fragrance Misty Records

— Original by Princess Deling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

When it was first reincarnated as a fox, it had nine tails, all of them very plump and beautiful... In addition, it could also use a magic of invisibility. In the end, it lost eight tails, but fortunately its precious invisibility magic was still preserved, so it was not completely useless. Originally, its nine tails were actually nine bad habits. Because it had these nine bad habits, it gradually became addicted, day by day falling, becoming a bad element between heaven and earth.

What were the nine bad habits? The first was liking to drink alcohol, often getting drunk; the second was recklessness and carelessness; the third was dishonesty, often lying and cheating; the fourth was greed for money, becoming envious when seeing precious things; the fifth was a quick temper; the sixth was gluttony, often stealing other people's food; the seventh was insatiable greed, wanting two when having one; the eighth was lust, always losing control when seeing beautiful women; the ninth was licentiousness, often indulging in excessive desire. These nine bad habits completely blinded its heart, and it was doing evil almost every day. Later, the Jade Emperor finally found out and was furious. He immediately took it away and severely rebuked it. Finally, he said, "From now on, you must reform and become a good fox! The only way now is to cut off one of your tails?" It was very anxious when it heard this, because it loved all nine of its tails. It didn't know which tail to remove to cause it the least amount of pain. However, the Jade Emperor did not allow it to have a choice and immediately issued an order to cut off the tail that made it like to drink alcohol. He repeatedly warned, "Now I will give you another thousand years to cultivate yourself and change your behavior." (204)

Places Visited

On the Road in Wuxi and Yixing

— Huoxue Ming

A desolate autumn rain, dampening the gloomy morning streets. I slipped out quietly from the Second Inn. The rickshaw pullers, seemingly unafraid of the wind and rain, swarmed over, calling out, "Sir, Zhaotouzhu? Oh, Xiaojishan?... Plum Garden?" Their voices had a hint of trembling and a touch of flippancy.

As usual, I shook my head, pulled up my collar, and walked onto the infinitely tranquil and cool Shima Road. Although I yearned for the Shuangdong Caves of Yixing, and thus summoned strong courage, it would not be the traveler's fortune if the rain grew heavier.

"But what's the point of staying in Wuxi city, watching the rain? Even if the rain gets heavier, I still have to go to Yixing." Finally, this is how I strengthened my wavering will.

I ate a bowl of soup noodles at a teahouse opposite the Jiangnan Automobile Company under Tongyun Bridge, bought a round-trip ticket for one yuan and ten cents to the station, boarded the fourth bus, and left the city at exactly seven o'clock. Passing Huangbu Pier in the northwest, so charmingly situated in the middle of the canal, with red walls peeking through the gaps in the weeping willows, and fishing sails flying in the water breeze, I instinctively thought of the Fengzi of the Nanhu Misty Rain Tower. Wasn't there a drizzle in the sky?

Our car darted into Rong Lane, the horn blaring continuously. The roof was almost level with the eaves of the houses on both sides, and the body of the car just barely cleared the steps on both sides. If it turned too fast, or if the pedestrians on the opposite side retreated a little slowly, I think it would be very easy to have a fatal accident here. It's fundamentally unsuitable to have traffic vehicles going back and forth on a small market street, and the street of this market is so narrow; I really can't figure out why the people of Rong Lane don't cherish their lives and oppose it!

In thirty minutes, we arrived at Plum Garden and stopped for a moment. That garden, which would be famous for its "fragrant snow sea" in a hundred more days, could not attract elegant people to tread the snow and seek poetry at this moment, and not even a single mountain bird could be heard in the dense foliage. From Yangwan to Xueyan Bridge, the car leaned against the mountains on the right, winding westward; the silvery light and shadow of Taihu Lake on the left, like flowing mercury, slightly brightened my melancholy eyes. The water hung in the sky, and the sky connected to the water, a vast expanse, without even a trace of light blue boundary that could be distinguished. The mountains in the lake, lying on white satin, embraced several charming snails, those yachts and awning boats, only as black as flies, crawling slowly.

This car is not only left lake and right mountain, but also the twists and turns up and down are severe. Often the car is close to the lake, and it seems that there is no way to go in front, but the peak turns and the path changes, and it immediately drives into the mountains, and the lake surface becomes far and small; not long after, the mountain path unfolds again, still sending the lake waves back. It's like a coiled long dragon, stretching its limbs, coiling down from the top of the mountain, and flying up from the lake. If you have taken the Fuyang Road car, from Fancun to the Liuhe Pagoda section; you will definitely say that the scenery here is very similar. But I think that the mountain colors and lake scenery of Erlongtou, because the Qiantang River is not as good as Taihu Lake, the greatness still belongs here.

West of Panjia Bridge, Taihu Lake left us and was no longer visible.

The mountain colors also lacked the shadows, not as lively and agile as before. But the rain had stopped, the clear clouds released blue, and the sun slowly brightened, shining on the pine forests and rocks densely covered with pearls, especially bright. Distant peaks and near peaks, in turn, poked their heads out from the silvery-gray mist. At the edge of the Heshui station, fishermen on the riverbank were wearing palm cloaks, drying wet nets, and some were holding fishing rods, staring intently as they spied on our car speeding by. It was truly a wonderful poem!

The villagers in the same car were very simple in their clothes. They would politely tell you which family's pottery from Dushan and tea from Mingling were the best; when the Tonghe Bridge traffic car to Changzhou could depart; but if you asked about Gengsang and Shanshan, they would all stare blankly and be unable to answer. The closer people are to the city, the less they have visited the scenery of their local area because of the burden of labor. This may also be due to different interests. Therefore, city people are particularly envious of the life of mountain people, and do not hesitate to travel far to climb peaks and explore caves; while the woodcutters and silkworm farmers, upon seeing the silk carriages and horses of city people, are also so envious!

Unconsciously, I spent the time of viewing the mountains in idle conversation. Suddenly, the passengers in the car became commotioned, all tidying up their luggage; looking up, I found another city moat, embracing the red-roofed station, with large characters clearly marked on the station building, indicating that Yixing had indeed arrived!

Education News

Full Text of Resolutions of the National Vocational Education Conference (II)

Case 6: Proposal on Promoting Agricultural Vocational Education

Scheme for Promoting Agricultural Vocational Education (Proposed by Jiang Wenyu et al., six persons)

Proposal for Improving China's Agricultural Education (Proposed by the Education Department of Henan Province)

Agricultural Vocational Schools Should Focus on Agricultural Extension and Guidance (Proposed by the Education Department of Anhui Province)

Request to Order All Provinces and Cities to Pay Special Attention to Agricultural Teaching and Practice for Rural Teachers and Rural Primary Schools as a Supplement to Promoting Agricultural Education (Proposed by the Education Department of Fujian Province)

Request the Ministry of Education to Issue a Circular to All Provinces and Cities to Establish Agricultural Instructor Training Classes as Soon as Possible to Relieve Rural Areas and Enrich Production (Proposed by the Education Department of Sichuan Province)

Resolution:

1. Principles for Promoting Agricultural Vocational Education:

(1) Vertical Aspect: Agricultural Education, Agricultural Affairs Education, and Farmer Education should have a consistent system.

(2) Horizontal Aspect: Agricultural Vocational Education should be integrated with Teacher Training and Social Education.

(3) The Cultivation of Agricultural Education Talents Should Adopt a Unified Method, with the Cooperation of Relevant Agencies in Each Province and City, and Managed by Educational Administrative Agencies.

2. Methods for Promoting Agricultural Vocational Education:

(1) Agricultural Education: The Original Agricultural Colleges or Agricultural Vocational Schools in Each City Should Conduct Systematic Research on Local Agricultural Products, Focusing on Practical Academic Problems such as Improving Varieties, Increasing Indigenous Products, Eliminating Pests, and Reducing Consumption. They Should Also Work on Solving Difficulties and Entrusted Experiments for Various Localities in Each Province and City. When Necessary, Short-Term Special Training Classes or Training Courses May Also Be Established. (2) Agricultural Affairs Education: Each Province and City Should Establish Senior and Junior Agricultural Vocational Schools Based on Local Needs, Enrolling Older Farmers' Children, or Those Who Have Interest and Experience in Agriculture, and Imparting Rigorous Agricultural Education. Emphasis Should Be Placed on Both Theory and Practice. Practice Should Involve Actual Labor and Technical Training. In the Future, the Goal Should Be to Effectively Guide Farmers to Improve Agriculture. Rural Normal Schools Should Also Pay Special Attention to Agricultural Teaching and Practice, and Teach Subjects such as Cooperation and Water Conservancy.

(3) Farmer Education: Each Province and City Should Directly Implement Farmer Education. The Methods Can Be Adapted to the Time and Place. The Following Methods Are Listed for Reference:

A. Each Province and City Should Select Suitable Locations to Conduct Rural Improvement Areas on a Trial Basis, Starting with Guiding Farmers to Increase Production, and Simultaneously Imparting Literacy, Hygiene, Baojia Cooperation, and Other Common Knowledge, and Organizing and Implementing Education, Cultivation, and Health Work on Their Behalf.

B. Each Province and City Should Use Existing or Newly Established Farmer Education Centers or Mass Education Centers as the Center for Promoting Farmer Education, with Graduates from Senior Agricultural Vocational Schools Who Have Received Civil Education Training or Civil Education Graduates Who Have Received Agricultural Training as Directors and Staff, Responsible for Introducing Varieties, Improving Agricultural Tools, Selecting Fertilizers, Promoting Side Businesses, and Organizing Cooperation in a County, Township, or Town, While Providing Literacy, Entertainment, and Other Convenience. C. Mobile Agricultural Spare-Time Schools Should Be Conducted by Graduates of Senior and Junior Agricultural Vocational Schools, Under the Guidance of Agricultural Colleges or Agricultural Vocational Schools, Going to Various Villages to Directly Guide Farmers to Impart Knowledge of Agricultural Science During Agricultural Spare Time, and to Teach Literacy and Civic Training.

D. Rural Teachers Should Promote Education: The Farmer Education in the Location of Rural Teachers Should Be Undertaken by the Rural Teachers, and the Rural Teachers Should Instruct the Attached Primary Schools or the Assisted Primary Schools to Pay Attention to Agricultural Teaching and Practice. When Necessary, Rural Primary Schools May Also Appropriately Increase the Number of Agricultural Teaching and Practice Hours, so That Farmers Can Receive Scientific Agricultural Knowledge from an Early Age.

E. Rural Primary Schools Must Pay Attention to the Vocational Development of Older Children, and at the Same Time, Divide the Area Near the School into an Improvement Zone, and Guide Farmers to Improve All Aspects of Life in Their Spare Time.

(4) The Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Industry Should Order the Education Departments or Bureaus of Each Province and City, the Social Bureaus, and the Construction Departments and Other Relevant Agencies to Cooperate Closely. All Public and Private Farms Should Provide Practice Sites for Nearby Agricultural Education Institutions. The Talent Needs of Agricultural Construction Should Be Statistically Determined in Advance, and the Quantity Should Be Determined. The Educational Administrative Agencies Should Be Responsible for Unified Cultivation, to Avoid Administrative System Chaos, and the Difficulty of Finding Employment for Agricultural Vocational School Graduates.

Case 7: Senior Vocational School Students Have Difficulties Due to Too Much Seasonal Internship and Centralized Military Training. It is Proposed to Exempt Centralized Military Training (Temporarily Proposed by Representatives of Various Provinces and Cities)

Resolution:

1. It is Proposed to Exempt First-Year Students of Senior Vocational Schools from Centralized Military Training.

2. It is Proposed that After the Exemption of Centralized Military Training, the Regular Military Training Should Be Extended to the Second Year to Supplement It. The Above Measures Should Be Approved and Implemented by the Ministry of Education in Consultation with the General Directorate of Training.

Case 8: Proposal on Inspecting and Reorganizing Vocational Schools

Each Province and City Should Promptly Reorganize or Enrich the Original Vocational Schools and Ban Bad Public and Private Vocational Schools (Proposed by the Ministry of Education)

Resolution:

1. Each Province and City Should Conduct a Thorough Inspection of the Actual Situation of Public and Private Vocational Schools in the Province and City, Assess Their Performance, and Report to the Ministry for Record.

2. Each Province and City Should Order Public and Private Vocational Schools That Are Poorly Run and Have Poor Performance to Improve Within a Time Limit. If They Cannot Improve After the Deadline, They Should Be Strictly Banned.

Case 9: Proposal on Vocational School Awards and Subsidies

The Central Government and Various Provinces and Cities Subsidize Excellent Vocational Schools (Proposed by the Ministry of Education) Please Forward the Motion to the Boxer Indemnity Custody Committee and the National Economic Committee to Allocate Funds to Subsidize the Equipment of Vocational Schools in Various Provinces and Cities, or to Establish Vocational Schools with Extremely Fixed Equipment in Important Cities and Towns and Rural Areas (Proposed by the Education Department of Hubei Province)

Request the Central Government to Appropriately Provide Funding to Reward Excellent Vocational Schools in Various Provinces and Cities (Proposed by the Director of the Education Department of Jiangsu Province)

Subsidizing Excellent Private Vocational Schools (Proposed by the Director of the Education Department of Hunan Province)

Regulations on the Reward Methods for Private Vocational Schools (Proposed by the Education Bureau of Shanghai Municipality)

Resolution:

1. Each Province and City Should Formulate Subsidy Methods and Allocate Funds Annually to Subsidize Public and Private Vocational Schools with Excellent Performance in the Province and City for Equipment Fees or Operating Expenses.

2. Based on the Inspection Results, the Ministry of Education Should Request the Central Government to Allocate Certain Funds Annually to Subsidize the Equipment Fees or Part of the Operating Expenses of Public and Private Vocational Schools with Excellent Performance Nationwide, and Formulate Subsidy Methods.

Case 10: Proposal on Vocational School Teachers and Treatment

Training Vocational School Teachers (Proposed by the Ministry of Education)

Request the Central Government to Centrally Train Vocational School Teachers to Meet the Needs of Various Provinces (Proposed by the Education Department of Fujian Province) The Treatment of Teachers of Vocational Subjects in Vocational Schools Should Be Explicitly Increased to Facilitate the Hiring of Skilled Technical Talents (Proposed by the Education Department of Hubei Province)

Request the Central Government to Establish a Vocational School Teacher Training Institution as Soon as Possible (Proposed by the Education Department of Hubei Province)

Request for the Cultivation of Teachers for Aquatic Vocational Schools (Proposed by Hou Zhaohai)

How Should Teachers of Vocational Supplementary Schools Be Trained? (Proposed by the Education Bureau of Shanghai Municipality)

Resolution:

1. Each Province and City Needs Teachers for Vocational Schools at All Levels. Based on the Actual Situation, First Determine the Types of Schools and Subjects, and Then Investigate the Types and Quantities of Teachers Lacking and Send a List to the Ministry.

2. Senior Vocational School Teacher Training Should Be Organized by the Central Government. The Implementation Details Will Be Formulated Separately.

3. Junior Vocational School Teacher Training Should Be Based on the Principle of Being Organized by Each Province and City. If Each Province and City Has Special Circumstances and Cannot Hold It, the Central Government Will Find a Way to Hold It or Entrust Another Province and City to Do It on Its Behalf.

4. Conduct Vocational Teacher Registration, Investigate Teachers Who Have Received Professional Training for the Purpose of Introduction.

Case 11: Proposal on the Employment Problems of Vocational School Graduates

Category A

Promoting the Employment of Vocational School Graduates (Proposed by the Education Department of Chahar Province)

Agricultural, Industrial, and Commercial Institutions Operated by the Government Should Allow Students and Graduates of Schools of the Same Nature to Intern and Serve to Encourage Them (Proposed by the Education Department of Hubei Province)

Regulations on the Use of Vocational School Graduates (Proposed by Li Fangyu, Representative of Shanxi)

Regarding the Raw Materials Produced in Jiangsu Province, Please Set Up Factories in the Central Government to Promote the Industry (Proposed by the Education Department of Jiangsu Province)

It is Proposed to Request the Central Government to Issue a Clear Order to National Construction Agencies to Employ Vocational School Graduates (Proposed by the Education Bureau of Shanghai Municipality)

(The Above Five Cases Are Discussed Together)

Resolution:

1. This Meeting Recommends That the Ministry of Education Submit a Report to the National Government, Ordering the National Economic Committee and the Ministry of Industry to Pay Attention to the Local Specialties of Various Provinces and Cities and Set Up Factories, Farms, and Pastures Separately to Enrich the People's Livelihood.

2. This Meeting Requests the National Government to Order the National Economic Committee, the Construction Committee, the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Communications, the Ministry of Railways, and the Ministry of Education to Jointly Form a Central Vocational Introduction Agency, or This Agency Should Be Attached to the National Academic Work Consulting Office to Jointly Plan the Employment of Vocational School Graduates. 3. This Meeting Requests the National Government to Issue a Clear Order to National Public Production Institutions and Administrative Agencies Related to Production That Their Technical and Management Personnel Should Give Priority to Graduates of Vocational Schools and Pay Special Attention to the Northwestern Provinces and Production Institutions, and Should Allow Students of Schools of the Same Nature to Intern as Much as Possible.

Category B

The Government Provides Loans to Vocational School Graduates to Engage in Production on the Ground (Proposed by the Education Department of Suiyuan Province)

Vocational Education and Production Guidance Should Be Advanced Simultaneously to Achieve Mutual Use (Proposed by He, Representative of Weihaiwei)

Counties and Cities Should Set Up Product Sales Centers for Vocational Schools to Encourage Production (Proposed by the Education Bureau of Shanghai Municipality)

(The Above Three Cases Are Discussed Together)

Resolution: The Three Departments of Construction, Education, and Finance of Each Province Should Jointly Organize a Loan Committee and a Vocational Introduction Agency, and Include the Original Proposal That Vocational Education and Production Guidance Should Be Advanced Simultaneously, for Reference by Each Province in Organizing This Agency.

(Jinan, 19th Dispatch) The students who went on strike and left the school at Yuying Middle School have all submitted letters of repentance and returned to school to resume classes. The disturbance is resolved.

Fudan High School Affiliated to Xujiahui

Lixuelou Hall to Hold Inauguration Ceremony This Morning

Since Mr. Yin Yiwen took over as the principal of Fudan High School Affiliated to Xujiahui, he has strived to expand the school. The original school buildings, which were the ancestral halls of the Li family, were not suitable for school use. Last autumn, a large sum of money was raised to construct new buildings, including the renovation of two dormitories and a library, as well as the construction of a new three-story building. This autumn, the buildings were completed, and they are spacious, magnificent, and extremely spectacular. They are now used as classrooms and offices and are named "Lixuelou" to commemorate Mr. Shao Lizi and his wife, Ms. Fu Xuewen, for their support of the affiliated high school. The inauguration ceremony is scheduled to be held today. In addition to Mr. and Mrs. Shao personally attending, celebrities and alumni have been invited to visit. The inauguration ceremony will be held at 9:30 am, followed by an inspection of the student army and Boy Scouts. A sports meeting and variety show will be held in the afternoon. The scene will be bustling with activity.

Innes Right Winger Suffers Leg Fracture

Unfortunate Incident During Friendly Football Match

Youyou Team Wins 5-2

The Youyou football team played a friendly match against Innes yesterday at Shen Garden. Although Youyou won 5-2, an unfortunate incident occurred. Innes' right winger, Maskersky, fractured his leg bone in an unintentional collision with Youyou defender Lu Zhiming in the tenth minute of the first half. He was taken to the British Army Hospital by emergency ambulance.

Tragic Incident Wu Shouheng was the referee. In the first ten minutes of the game, Innes' offense was strong, pressing repeatedly. Youyou suffered due to the lack of strict midfield defense. However, Innes' forwards lacked accuracy and shot the ball wide of the goal. Otherwise, Youyou would have been in trouble. At about the tenth minute, Innes' right winger Maskersky dribbled the ball from the right. Lu Zhiming rushed to defend. In that instant, the two collided with a crisp sound that could be heard throughout the field. Maskersky fell to the ground. It was clear that his leg bone was broken. An ambulance was called urgently to treat him. Innes was replaced by Xun Jinno. The game was paused for over ten minutes.

Youyou Wins Play continued, and Youyou's defense avoided danger, conceding slightly. In the siege, Innes' Cullen first headed in a goal to open the scoring. Zhong Yongshen retaliated, making it 1-1. Cullen headed in again, giving Innes a 2-1 lead in the first half. In the second half, Youyou's two main defenders, Jiang Wang, entered the game. With a solid defense, they were able to attack at will. The second half was dominated by Youyou. Xi Qiaosheng crossed the ball, and Wang Caigao flicked it in, tying the score. Zhong Yongshen scored again, giving Youyou a 3-2 lead. Sun Jinshun scored, making it 4-2. Finally, Hu Youcheng scored, ending the game 5-2. The weather was cold and gloomy yesterday, and there were few spectators. The lineups were as follows:

Financial Matters

Silver Price Falls, Pure Gold Rises

Spot Gold Recovers Two Yuan and Eight Jiao

Many Speculators Closing Positions, Prices Rise Then Fall

Although the gold market recovered yesterday, the overall trend in the first half of the day was not very strong. This was mainly because Finance Minister Kong dispelled rumors of inflation, and many speculators rushed to close their positions. As a result, prices initially rose but then fell. Although there were several rebounds midway, these were due to the efforts of Chinese banks to support foreign exchange, leading to tight domestic markets. In the morning, overseas silver markets in both England and America fell, and forward silver prices also decreased by 0.5 to 0.65 cents. Exchange rates slightly recovered, and London raw gold rose by 2 pence. This naturally boosted confidence, and pre-market trading opened, briefly rising to 0.045. However, due to reports of Finance Minister Kong's refutation of the rumors, speculators took profits and closed positions, and large investors also took the opportunity to sell. This led to an oversupply and a sharp decline, falling below the 1,000 yuan mark. Selling pressure increased, and the Central Bank announced its exchange rates, with the British pound unchanged and the US dollar rising by 0.0625. Customs gold unit rose by 0.3 cents, and the standard gold price was listed as 1,005 yuan and 8 jiao. Prices stabilized slightly after the initial drop. After a high opening in the morning, prices were immediately pulled up, but suppliers were still active, and the market situation was quite volatile. Nevertheless, the overall trend continued to be positive, with demand exceeding supply. It was anticipated that the Hongkong and Shanghai Banking Corporation (HSBC) would announce exchange rates, with the British pound decreasing by 0.125 and the US dollar decreasing by 0.25. Subsequently, prices rose to the 1,000 yuan mark twice, but were obstructed due to eager supply. The struggle was intense. Then, the Central Bank and other banks vigorously supported the market, leading to a tight domestic market and rising prices. However, breaking through the 1,000 yuan mark proved difficult. Unexpectedly, after the rise was thwarted, a decline ensued. Dealers sold foreign exchange, and the market again showed an oversupply. Large investors supplied slightly, and speculators, already fatigued, suddenly started selling, leading to an immediate decline. However, Chinese banks again supported the market by purchasing exchange bills, and prices stabilized after the drop. Large investors bought at lower prices, while the silver equalization tax was announced to be reduced by 0.5 cents, levying only 6%. The exchange rate for the British pound, calculated at 1 shilling and 5 pence and 128125, initially rose but then fell back. Soon after, Chinese banks showed strong appetite, and the Central Bank, Bank of Communications, and others continued to buy, tightening the exchange market again. Buyers flocked in. Foreign wire reports indicated that the US was not entirely in agreement with granting loans to China. In addition, the Guangdong group continued to purchase aggressively, pushing prices up to the 1,000 yuan mark again. Supply at higher prices has not dissipated and prices are falling back again. The struggle was particularly strong in the middle. Later, when the exchange market stabilized, large investors and buyers waited and watched, and speculators panicked again. Selling activity ensued, so although buyers tried to purchase at lower prices, they could not temporarily raise prices. Due to the disparity between buyers and sellers, the market continued to fall at noon closing, and the swap rate had retreated to a premium of 12.5 yuan for short positions. As a result, it rose by 2 yuan and 5 jiao compared to the previous day. The trade volume was 105,000 jiao in the morning market and 40,000 jiao in the afternoon market. Copper coins were 300,000 "wen", which was 4,000 "wen" less than the previous day. The transaction amount was 29,400 "chuan wen", equivalent to 9,800 yuan.

Securities

Tight Monetary Conditions Make It Difficult for Public Bonds to Rally

Yesterday, the Shanghai Chinese Merchantile Securities Exchange market once again turned bearish. The so-called rumors of currency devaluation and paper money policies had been swept away. This is because China's financial situation is completely different from that of other countries. In fact, it is absolutely impossible at present. The securities market is overly sensitive, and rumors rise and fall easily. The high price of foreign short-term financing at 0.35 and "Hua Tou" at 0.40 shows that there has been no turnaround in monetary conditions. The financial sector is shorting shillings but not public bonds, causing the market to struggle. The huge amount of short positions previously released was only slightly offset the day before yesterday. Judging by the situation, most of them are preparing to be delivered. However, because the difference between near-term and long-term is too large, speculative trading is still active, so market prices fluctuate erratically. Yesterday, at the opening of the morning session, prices fell across the board due to the high price of foreign short-term financing. Issues 4 and 11, etc., were sold off, and the retail long positions were also poorly managed. Market prices fell sharply by 0.1-0.2 yuan to 1.1 yuan. The second session slightly offset the losses, rising by about 0.2-0.3 yuan. In the afternoon, it was heard that "Hua Tou" was trading at 0.40, and sentiment remained weak. Issues 17 and 53 continued to be sold off, and prices fell again by 0.3-0.5 yuan. At the close, issue 16 slightly offset the losses, and there were also temporary transactions to close positions on the trading floor, slightly rising by 0.2-0.3 yuan. Due to the approaching settlement date, market prices are expected to fluctuate. Yesterday's market prices fell by 0.3-0.4 yuan to 1.1-1.5 yuan. The total trading volume was 21.37 million yuan. The results of the gains and losses are listed in the comparison table on the left (unit: yuan, transaction unit: 100 yuan).

Sudden Decline in US Silver Stocks

Xinfeng Foreign Firm reported that yesterday (18th) the New York stock market was mixed, with the feature being the decline in silver stocks. It was found that silver stocks did not have any special pressure, and the decline was entirely affected by the decline in silver prices in New York, Montreux, and London. The drop in silver prices was due to the rumor that the United States had stopped purchasing due to a large number of sales. At the same time, rumors that China may reduce the fineness of silver dollars, although denied by semi-official sources, also contributed to the decline in silver prices, and the currencies of Shanghai and "Manchukuo" were affected. Also, news from Washington said that Treasury officials were unwilling to discuss reports of the United States stopping silver purchases in London, and reiterated that government silver purchasing activities must be kept extremely secret to avoid a huge storm in the market. According to private estimates, the US silver reserve is still 100 million ounces short of the legal amount. London silver circles believe that the above report is inaccurate, saying that they know that the United States purchased silver today. The bond market was mixed, with a total of 820,000 shares traded throughout the day. The Dow Jones index is listed on the left.

Yarn Market

Inflation is Active Again

Many Yarn Merchants' Courage Strengthened

Yarn Market's Rising Trend Starts Slightly, Although news agencies and authorities have firmly denied the matter of inflation, anxiety has resurfaced in the market, and rumors are spreading, including talk of Japanese merchants shorting the market. Consequently, buying interest has increased slightly, and yarn sales are still manageable. Under these chaotic circumstances, the yarn market's future lacks certainty.

"Golden Rooster" Recovers to Rise Six, Seven, Eight Jiao. The "Standard Yarn" market opened higher due to various rumors favoring bullish sentiment, leading to a decrease in sellers. On the 17th, Da Feng Company purchased aggressively to cover short positions, buying over two thousand bales, allegedly to cover a certain merchant's short squeeze. The market trended upward, and sentiment tightened. Consequently, prices for all months rose by seven or eight jiao. The afternoon opening was slightly weak, but prices rebounded strongly at the three o'clock closing. Current yarn sales are reportedly still good, with prices for all months only falling by one jiao. Sales included 2,100 bales from Jin Chang, 400 from Jun Chang, 1,250 from Tai Chang, 950 from Chang Feng, 550 from Sheng Yuan, 550 from Geng Feng, 1,250 from Run Kang, 600 from Yong Da, and 600 from Xin Cheng. Purchases included 800 bales from Sui Long, 2,500 from Da Feng, 700 from Geng Feng, 1,700 from Shen Chang, 1,300 from Heng Yi, 500 from Ren Feng, 900 from De Ji, and 1,350 from Tong Feng. Zheng Biao Recovers by Three Jiao. The "Standard Cotton" market opened higher, as U.S. cotton prices rose by five points, while Indian cotton fell by 0.25 to 1 rupee. U.S. Cotton Drops in Near Term, Rises in Far Term

Yesterday, the U.S. cotton market opened with prices fluctuating by two points. Bullish players in the December contract, having received delivery notices for 900 bales, closed their positions. However, due to limited trading, the market was firm. Traders made slight purchases, while Southern sellers were scarce, and cotton hoarders did not sell. Buyers feared that higher prices would trigger renewed selling and remained cautious. Eventually, local traders covered short positions, pushing prices up by four to seven points for all months, except for December, which rose by two points. Current cotton demand is weak, and the yarn and fabric market is stable and firm. Liverpool reported small trades, with most of the resales being absorbed by Bombay traders and traders. Spot prices rose by five points, while futures prices fluctuated from a decrease of two points to an increase of nine points. English cotton spot prices fell by three points, and futures prices fell by one to two points. Indian cotton prices were weak due to selling by European exporters and speculators. Pingle fell by 0.25 rupee, Omra fell by 1 rupee, and White Raw Creek fell by 0.75 rupee. Original telegram on the left (dated 18th).

Grains

Spot Flour Slightly Drops, Distant Months Weaker

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the market for each month generally showed a trend of stable near-term and weak distant-term contracts. As for imported wheat quotes, Chicago was up four fen to one jiao, and Canada was up one and a half jiao. At the opening, the spot month was quite active due to some buying by traders, so the market was stable. For distant months, large bullish players were inactive, and some were closing positions, so sentiment was weak for a time, falling one to two fen compared to the previous day's closing. By the afternoon opening, the spot month remained stable due to trader activity, while the factories continued selling distant months, causing the market situation to rebound slightly, rising more than a fen from the morning. Looking at the future market situation, it depends on the alignment of imported wheat prices; otherwise, it must be held steady. In the end, the spot month was up half a fen, January and February were up two and a half li, March was up seven and a half li, April was up half a fen, and May was up two and a half li.

Wheat Futures Quiet with a Hint of Weakness

Yesterday, the wheat futures market was generally quiet and weak in the morning and afternoon openings. As for imported wheat quotes, Chicago was up four fen to one jiao, and Canada was up around one and a half jiao. At the opening, trading in each month was still quiet. The spot month, due to the approaching delivery date and limited outstanding contracts, showed no intention of buying back by hedgers, so the situation was quiet with a hint of weakness. Distant months saw little buying, so fluctuations were minimal. This situation is due to the approaching Lunar New Year, and trading between Shanghai and customers has been virtually halted, so there are few major changes expected in the future. In the end, the spot month was down three fen from the previous day, January was down one fen, February was up one fen, and there were no changes in the rest. Spot wheat prices are holding steady due to inactivity from factories.

Chicago wheat market absorbed a large amount of selling, but unless there is an improvement in foreign demand, new purchases may not be sufficient to raise prices.

National Product Trademark

— Yang An

It is very difficult to distinguish between national products and non-national products. The most effective way to make it clear at a glance is the trademark. In general, a product that can gain the trust of society depends on the excellence of its manufacture and the low price. However, what makes people remember it forever is the established trademark. The key points of a trademark are: (1) It should be simple and easy to distinguish, so that people can understand it at a glance. (2) It should be popular and easy to understand, so that even women and children can understand it. (3) It should be interesting, so that people do not forget it. It is even more valuable if it can show the advantages of the product and promote the characteristics of national products. In the past, national product manufacturers, in order to cater to customers' preference for foreign goods, often used foreign languages ​​for Chinese national products. This not only lost the dignity of national products, but also made it easier for those who wanted to use national products to be confused, causing a problem of not knowing what to do. At this time when the national patriotic psychology is extremely developed and everyone is happy to use national products, it seems that there is no need to use foreign languages ​​to confuse the people. The characteristics of the product should be announced to the society through trademarks at any time, so that sellers know what to choose and users know what to ask. Factories in Europe, America and Japan hold competitions and exhibitions every month. Therefore, when people in their countries adopt goods, they have a clear idea in their minds and do not have to ask questions. There is the convenience of designation, and the development of national products has a long history. Manufacturers in our country are confused by short-term benefits and spare small expenses. They do not pay attention to the promotion of such trademarks, nor do they pay attention to the display of goods. They even use sub-brands and inferior goods to lower their credibility. This is a huge hidden reef for the future of national products. Recently, the Women's National Product Year Movement Committee held a national product trademark exhibition, collecting trademarks from various factories for public display, so that those who like to use certain products can strengthen their beliefs. The meaning is profound and valuable. It is deeply hoped that all national product manufacturers will pay more attention to the use of trademarks in the future, in order to maintain the dignity of their products, and to improve their products and reduce costs to be welcomed by the society. This is what the reporter sincerely hopes.

National Product Talk

Hopes for the Student National Product Year

— Ba Ling

This year's Women's National Product Year is about to

separate from us! Next year will be designated as the "Student National Product Year." What a "Student National Product Year!" Although I have been away from student life for a long time, I absolutely agree with it. I think: all the young compatriots who are studying must be very happy and express 120,000 points of agreement when they hear this news.

As the Student National Product Year is coming, I dare to, as a youth, make an earnest request to the generally respectable and lovable student comrades, what kind of request? Please listen to me:

(1) It is hoped that students will make a decision to use national products from now on: Students are the pillars of the country, the center of society, and the saviors of the nation. Of course, it is hoped that students will bear the responsibility of saving the country and the nation. It is also hoped that students will work hard to promote national products. If 80% of the students in the country can faithfully use national products and promote national products, and at the same time, recognize the use of foreign products as the greatest shame in life, then China's national product movement will definitely get a lot of help, unlimited promotion, and great achievements. Therefore, I very much hope that all young students in China will swear to use national products and promote national products from now on, so that the national product movement can achieve extraordinary results under the efforts of students, show that the spirit of the students is extraordinary, and at the same time, it can also correct the general perception that students are foreign product promoters.

(2) It is hoped that students can organize small groups for using national products, so as to achieve mutual supervision: I very much hope that when the Student National Product Year begins, students in each school will start to form small groups for using national products, whether it is a group of five people or a group of ten people, ask teachers to be instructors, and the group should formulate methods for using national products, publicizing the principles of national products, and supervising each other and encouraging efforts. Now, we can start preparing immediately and start forming the groups on New Year's Day. I think: This is also a very meaningful job.

(3) It is hoped that teachers will often encourage students: The quality of all students' achievements is closely related to teachers. Similarly, if we want the Student National Product Year to be effective, teachers must also take the responsibility of encouraging students. Although I do not study education, I know very well that students like to be rewarded by their teachers. Teachers should use this psychology to encourage students to use national products. The school may also organize a "Committee for Rewarding Students for Using National Products" to preside over this work. This is a very valuable and meaningful work. All schools in the country can try it out, which is closely related to the country and the nation.

The above three are what I hope for the upcoming Student National Product Year. I don't know if it can arouse the sympathy of all the young student comrades and teachers?

Talk About Commercial Competition

— Yang Chonggao

The rapid influx of foreign goods and the increasing number of foreign merchants

, Chinese merchants should wake up suddenly. In this era of "competition is the life of commerce," merchants in this situation must have the intelligence of competition, understand the psychology of competition, and know how to use the skills of competition. Only in this way can business prosper and avoid decline and elimination.

It is impossible for us to give a formula for competition, and it is even more impossible for us to use "competition is the life of commerce" to solve all commercial problems. We must understand that competition can make commercial life grow and also make commercial life die. This depends entirely on whether the application of competition is proper in the development of commerce.

In recent years, with the panic of social economy and the recession of all businesses, the path taken by the Chinese business community has gone downhill, and it can be said that it has completely gone astray. Everyone does not seek salvation through proper methods to solve the current crisis, but is only seeking temporary peace by playing with deceptive means. However, magic lanterns are always easy to see through, and at that time, we will be at the end of our rope.

The business community must know that competitors should compete with each other within their capabilities under the principle of the system to be reasonable and to seek excellence. We must also have the spirit of honesty丨丨"designated prices" and "genuine goods at fair prices"丨丨scientific minds and artistic selection are also indispensable.

If you want to rely on cunning "big sales," "full size plus three," "willing to lose money big sale" ... to use deceptive and false means to compete, then you can say without hesitation, "the dead end is right in front of you."

It is hoped that the business community will embark on the path of honest competition from now on, broaden their horizons, and first enrich their lineup丨丨do their best to promote national products and supervise the manufacturers' products丨丨compete rationally and profitably in the big market, and express their proper competition.

National Product Discussion

A Review of Opening Up Foreign Markets

— Xuan Wan

This may be my extravagant hope. In such a precarious future for national products, when the general production industry is clamoring about weak sales, stockpiling of inventory, and the difficulty of resisting imported goods and revitalizing national products, I actually want to go a step further and raise the issue of "exploring foreign market research." "Fool's dream" seems to be an impossible thing, but on closer inspection, it is not entirely so. This is precisely our good opportunity. Assuming that we can strive to move forward in the spirit of "selling one more point of national products is to increase the country's vitality by one point" and formulate a strict and precise plan, then it will always gradually approach our hopes and ideals.

We know that in the past and present, there are many overseas compatriots who are very eager for the motherland and demand national products. Song, the Consul General in Batavia, Dutch East Indies, and Mr. Huang Manshi, the representative of the Singapore Chamber of Commerce, both came to Shanghai this time, and both of them sincerely expressed their hope for the national product industry in our country. Therefore, our participation in the Philippine Carnival and the preparation for the large-scale Singapore National Exhibition have indeed become the first steps in promoting national products overseas recently. However, in addition to striving to fulfill this pioneering task, I feel that there are several fundamental problems that need to be urgently resolved and implemented. Now, I will put forward the three most worthy of discussion:

(1) Improvement of export goods and promotion of new export goods. In this era of fierce global industrial competition, the first element for us to develop international trade is, of course, to improve old products, and to widely observe the needs of various countries, and to promote a wide variety of new export goods, so as to improve technology, refine products, reduce manufacturing costs, and reduce prices, making them easy to promote.

(2) Tax-free exports and controlled export trade. The high tariff barriers built by various countries at present are indeed a major problem for the export of national products. Therefore, the first step we need at present should be tax-free exports from the government, and then we can contact the government to jointly establish a large-scale export trading company to comprehensively manage the export goods of our country and add reasonable control. We will determine the business principles at any time with specific plans and seek to open up foreign markets as a whole.

(3) Various technical issues during export. Like how to package export goods, the procedures for shipping and bank mortgage, the budget for exchange rate abuses, the preparation of product samples, advertising and sales methods, we have rarely studied these many technical issues during export in the past, so we must first consider them now before we can easily start.

In addition, we should also know that the current government also has this new tendency. The International Trade Bureau is also convening manufacturers of national products from various countries to discuss ways to help promote sales, and it is also the time when Japanese goods are encountering obstacles everywhere. Therefore, this is a good opportunity given to us by nature, and we must take the opportunity to work hard and never miss it!

National Product News

National Product Trademark Sample Exhibition

— Sun Choucheng

The Women's National Product Year Movement Committee of this city, in view of the imminent end of the Women's National Product Year, specially held a National Product Trademark Sample Exhibition at the Dacheng Hall of the People's Education Hall on Wenmiao Road in Nanshi. To promote national development, we must first enable the general public to recognize national products, so that they will not be deceived by unscrupulous merchants and mistakenly purchase foreign goods when purchasing goods. In the past, various national product exhibitions have focused on the product aspect and did not pay much attention to trademarks. As a result, there have been many cases where compatriots who love to use national products, after purchasing and using them once, want to purchase the product a second time, but cannot repurchase it because they forget the trademark. Therefore, this time, the trademark and the sample are listed at the same time, so that visitors can easily remember them. The method is good and the meaning is beautiful and worthy of learning. The next day, the newspapers were limited in space and only published a general situation. Therefore, I will not hesitate to record the details that were not detailed in the newspapers as follows: The exhibition period is from December 14th to 16th, a total of three days. Choucheng went there at 10:00 am on the first morning and saw the Party and National flags intersecting in the shape of a transaction under the plaque of the "Sacrificial Confucius Instrument Display Office", and a white cloth banner with the words "National Product Trademark Sample Exhibition Display Office" was hung on the facade. He met Mr. Ni Baiyan, an officer of the association, who led him to visit the exhibition. He spoke very modestly, saying that the decision to display the trademark and the sample in the same place this time was to make it easier for visitors to identify and remember. The types of exhibits were stipulated in advance, and each factory designed its own products and brought products with its own trademark, marking the price, brand name, raw material composition and usage instructions, etc., to the meeting for registration, and then arranged them in order, designated the location, and sent personnel to the venue to arrange them by themselves to show fairness. The pillars were covered with slogans such as "Sir, look at their family. Aren't they all using national products?" and "If it's not a national product, the more gorgeous it is, the more shameful it is." In front of the Confucius shrine, long tables were built with wooden boards, covered with tablecloths, and the trademark samples were displayed in a designated position, competing for beauty, all using artistic methods to attract people. For example, the China National Products Company embroidered its trademark on a light yellow plain satin that was a foot and a half wide and three feet long, with tassels hanging down, and hung it high above the glass cabinet of the ritual instrument. It was the most eye-catching thing when you entered the door. The small steel piano it produced on the table was only a foot square. When pressed, it made a clang sound, with ups and downs, and it was just like a piano. Next to the electric fan of the Yabuer Electric Appliance Factory, there was a square plate with various light bulbs inserted on it, which could be used to test the height of the power and the size of the light. It was sometimes bright and sometimes dark, and everyone paid attention to it. In addition to drawing a green water and white goose backdrop and hanging it high under the vermilion plaque of "Sacred God Tianzong," the Wuhe Weaving Factory also put the goose brand cotton wool shirts and health shirts it produced on wooden racks, arranged in order according to their size. From a distance, it was like a horizontal team formed by elementary school students during gymnastics. In addition to displaying various candies, the Guanshengyuan also placed the "Life" trademark on the top of the cabinet, and enlarged the photo of Ms. Ren Xiuqun, a patriotic female student who likes to eat butter toffee, and placed it next to the table, holding a bag of candy with a sweet and innocent smile, which was very lifelike. Female students stopped and looked at it carefully and were reluctant to leave, causing the viewers to be like walls. Other examples include the various silk samples of the Mei Ya Silk Weaving Factory, which were colorful, and the electric wood and electric jade appliances of the Ya Guang Manufacturing Company, which were smooth, clean and beautiful. I can't list them all in detail. In short, various goods are no less than the same imported goods. I hope that all of you who visit the exhibition will remember the trademarks and purchase them for trial use, so as not to fail the intention of the association in holding this exhibition.

Short Stories

Santa Claus's Gift

— Rong Yu

The revolving years have once again turned to winter. The cold wind is blowing fiercely, causing people to shrink their necks and put their hands in their sleeves; causing the trees to be bald and bare; causing the sun to be dim and unable to emit its usual majesty; causing the sky to be covered with dark clouds, as if brewing for snow. Blowing and blowing, bringing a foreign festival, Christmas, 丨a foreign winter solstice丨.

Huang Dafang, that little child, is only eleven years old, has already finished primary school, and is now in the first grade of senior primary school. His parents are Christians, so on the night before Christmas, they buy some expensive gifts for him. They don't let Dafang know beforehand. While he is fast asleep that night, they put the things in a large stocking. Edibles like chocolate candies, coffee candies, milk candies; toys like foreign dolls, small cars, small airplanes, everything is available. They hang this stocking on top of Dafang's bed. When Dafang wakes up, his eyes still drowsy, he sees this bag of gifts. He jumps up with joy, holding the bag of gifts, deliberately asking, "Who gave me this lovely gift?" His mother replies, "Santa Claus." Dafang asks again, "What kind of person is Santa Claus?" His mother says again, "He is an old man wearing a large robe, a pointed hat, and snow-white hair." Dafang says again, "Mom! When this old man came, why didn't he wake me up and let me see his face; and personally thank him!" His mother chuckles and says, "There's no need for you to thank him. We have already thanked him for you!" Year after year, Dafang also knows that this is a trick of his parents, but he doesn't expose it, in order to please his parents. These few days, Dafang knows that his parents are preparing his Christmas gifts again, so he says to his parents, "These two years are the years of national products. What we eat, wear, and use should all be national products. Even the toys we children play with should also be national products. The teacher at school also told us: This year, because there are many unpatriotic children who do not use national products, just the import of toys alone has already amounted to several hundred thousand yuan. In this way, we children also have a share of the responsibility for China's poverty! Moreover, next year is designated as the Student National Products Year. I am a member of the primary school students. If I still play with imported toys and eat imported candies, it will not only be a loss of the personality of a dignified Chinese citizen; but also a black sheep, punishable by everyone丨So this year, if Santa Claus sends me national product gifts, I will not only thank him for his kindness; but also treat it as a souvenir of sincere use of national products. If he still sends me the previous imported goods, I will throw this thing in the trash can!" His parents nodded repeatedly upon hearing these words, praising him for his true ambition.

In the blink of an eye, Christmas Eve arrived, and Dafang still slept peacefully in his bed, just like last year. Tomorrow he will wake up, and a bag of gifts will be next to him. He opens it and sees a set of student attire, produced by the Sanyou Industrial Company; and many candies, all produced by Guanshengyuan and Taifeng Companies. He is extremely happy to see them. Below many things, there is also a card attached, with a few lines written on it: "These national product gifts are for my patriotic

student Huang Dafang, from a patriotic Santa Claus."
